int f(int a, int b) {
    return a + b;

program34.c

Lexer: OK Parser: OK
Source Code 
int main(void) {
    int x;
    for (x = 0; x < 10; x = x + 1) {
        int y;
        y = 5;
    }
    y = 10;
    return y;
}
